I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Signed-Releases check ignores .sigstore.json signatures produced by sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python
**Describe the bug**
The `Signed-Releases` check currently checks for:
> ...the following filenames in the project's last five release assets: *.minisig, *.asc (pgp), *.sig, *.sign, *.sigstore, *.intoto.jsonl.

For Python packages, the easiest way to create sigstore signatures is with the [sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python](https://github.com/sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python) GitHub Action. The GitHub Action's implementation when signing blobs produces a `.sigstore.json` file.

Since `.sigstore.json` does not match any of the file patterns in the `Signed-Releases` check, Python projects using this GitHub Action show up as failing the check when they do have valid sigstore signatures for their releases.

**Reproduction steps**
Steps to reproduce the behavior:
1. Run `scorecard --repo https://github.com/mark-adams/python-test-groups`
2. Observe that the `Signed-Releases` check has a score of 0.
3. Visit https://github.com/mark-adams/pytest-test-groups/releases/tag/1.2.1 (the latest release)
4. Observe that `.sigstore.json` files are present for all *.tar.gz and *.whl artifacts.

**Expected behavior**
Since these sigstore signatures are produced with the official sigstore GitHub Action, I would expect that the `Signed-Releases` check should have a score of 8 since sigstore signatures are present for the artifacts in each release.


</pr_description>

    54	        }

    56	        // Return the score evaluation.

    20	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
    21	)
    22	
    23	// SignedReleases checks for presence of signed release check.
    24	func SignedReleases(c *checker.CheckRequest) (checker.SignedReleasesData, error) {
    25	        releases, err := c.RepoClient.ListReleases()
    26	        if err != nil {
    27	                return checker.SignedReleasesData{}, fmt.Errorf("%w", err)
    28	        }
    29	
    30	        pkgs := []checker.ProjectPackage{}
    31	        versions, err := c.ProjectClient.GetProjectPackageVersions(c.Ctx, c.Repo.Host(), c.Repo.Path())
    32	        if err != nil {
    33	                if c.Dlogger != nil {
    34	                        c.Dlogger.Debug(&checker.LogMessage{Text: fmt.Sprintf("GetProjectPackageVersions: %v", err)})
    35	                }
    36	                return checker.SignedReleasesData{
    37	                        Releases: releases,
    38	                        Packages: pkgs,
    39	                }, nil
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        for _, v := range versions.Versions {
    43	                prov := checker.PackageProvenance{}
    44	
    45	                if len(v.SLSAProvenances) > 0 {
    46	                        prov = checker.PackageProvenance{
    47	                                Commit:     v.SLSAProvenances[0].Commit,
    48	                                IsVerified: v.SLSAProvenances[0].Verified,
    49	                        }
    50	                }
    51	
    52	                pkgs = append(pkgs, checker.ProjectPackage{
    53	                        System:     v.VersionKey.System,
    54	                        Name:       v.VersionKey.Name,
    55	                        Version:    v.VersionKey.Version,
    56	                        Provenance: prov,
    57	                })
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        return checker.SignedReleasesData{
    61	                Releases: releases,
    62	                Packages: pkgs,
    63	        }, nil
    64	}
    65

    16	package releasesAreSigned
    17	
    18	import (
    19	        "embed"
    20	        "fmt"
    21	        "strings"
    22	
    23	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
    24	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/finding"
    25	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/checknames"
    26	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/internal/probes"
    27	        "github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/internal/utils/uerror"
    28	)
    29	
    30	func init() {
    31	        probes.MustRegister(Probe, Run, []checknames.CheckName{checknames.SignedReleases})
    32	}
    33	
    34	//go:embed *.yml
    35	var fs embed.FS
    36	
    37	const (
    38	        Probe           = "releasesAreSigned"
    39	        ReleaseNameKey  = "releaseName"
    40	        AssetNameKey    = "assetName"
    41	        releaseLookBack = 5
    42	)
    43	
    44	var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore"}
    45	
    46	func Run(raw *checker.RawResults) ([]finding.Finding, string, error) {
    47	        if raw == nil {
    48	                return nil, "", fmt.Errorf("%w: raw", uerror.ErrNil)
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        var findings []finding.Finding
    52	
    53	        releases := raw.SignedReleasesResults.Releases
    54	
    55	        totalReleases := 0
    56	        for releaseIndex, release := range releases {
    57	                if releaseIndex >= releaseLookBack {
    58	                        break
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if len(release.Assets) == 0 {
    62	                        continue
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                totalReleases++
    66	                signed := false
    67	                for j := range release.Assets {
    68	                        asset := release.Assets[j]
    69	                        for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
    70	                                if !strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
    71	                                        continue
    72	                                }
    73	                                // Create True Finding
    74	                                // with file info
    75	                                loc := &finding.Location{
    76	                                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
    77	                                        Path: asset.URL,
    78	                                }
    79	                                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
    80	                                        fmt.Sprintf("signed release artifact: %s", asset.Name),
    81	                                        loc,
    82	                                        finding.OutcomeTrue)
    83	                                if err != nil {
    84	                                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
    85	                                }
    86	                                f.Values = map[string]string{
    87	                                        ReleaseNameKey: release.TagName,
    88	                                        AssetNameKey:   asset.Name,
    89	                                }
    90	                                findings = append(findings, *f)
    91	                                signed = true
    92	                                break
    93	                        }
    94	                        if signed {
    95	                                break
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                if signed {
    99	                        continue
   100	                }
   101	
   102	                // Release is not signed
   103	                loc := &finding.Location{
   104	                        Type: finding.FileTypeURL,
   105	                        Path: release.URL,
   106	                }
   107	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   108	                        fmt.Sprintf("release artifact %s not signed", release.TagName),
   109	                        loc,
   110	                        finding.OutcomeFalse)
   111	                if err != nil {
   112	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   113	                }
   114	                f = f.WithValue(ReleaseNameKey, release.TagName)
   115	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if len(findings) == 0 {
   119	                f, err := finding.NewWith(fs, Probe,
   120	                        "no GitHub/GitLab releases found",
   121	                        nil,
   122	                        finding.OutcomeNotApplicable)
   123	                if err != nil {
   124	                        return nil, Probe, fmt.Errorf("create finding: %w", err)
   125	                }
   126	                findings = append(findings, *f)
   127	        }
   128	        return findings, Probe, nil
   129	}
   130

"""Test script to verify sigstore.json detection functionality."""

import os

def test_extensions():
    # Current signature extensions from the code
    current_extensions = [".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore"]
    
    # Test files with different signature formats
    test_files = [
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.minisig", 
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sign",
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore",
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json",  # This should be detected but currently isn'"'"'t
        "package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json",     # This should be detected but currently isn'"'"'t
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz",                # Not a signature file
        "package-1.0.0.whl",                    # Not a signature file
    ]
    
    print("Testing current signature extension detection:")
    print("Current extensions:", current_extensions)
    print()
    
    for test_file in test_files:
        is_signature = False
        for ext in current_extensions:
            if test_file.endswith(ext):
                is_signature = True
                break
        
        status = "✓ SIGNATURE" if is_signature else "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
        print(f"{test_file:50} {status}")
    
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    
    # Test with proposed fix
    proposed_extensions = current_extensions + [".sigstore.json"]
    print("\nTesting with proposed fix (adding .sigstore.json):")
    print("Proposed extensions:", proposed_extensions)
    print()
    
    for test_file in test_files:
        is_signature = False
        for ext in proposed_extensions:
            if test_file.endswith(ext):
                is_signature = True
                break
        
        status = "✓ SIGNATURE" if is_signature else "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
        print(f"{test_file:50} {status}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_extensions()'

   236	func release(version string) clients.Release {
   237	        return clients.Release{
   238	                TagName:         version,
   239	                URL:             fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/test_artifact/releases/tag/%s", version),
   240	                TargetCommitish: "master",
   241	                Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
   242	                        {
   243	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_checksums.txt", version),
   244	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_checksums.txt", version, version),
   245	                        },
   246	                        {
   247	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_checksums.txt.sig", version),
   248	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_checksums.txt.sig", version, version),
   249	                        },
   250	                        {
   251	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_darwin_x86_64.tar.gz", version),
   252	                                URL:  fmt.Sprintf("https://github.com/test/repo/releases/%s/%s_darwin_x86_64.tar.gz", version, version),
   253	                        },
   254	                        {
   255	                                Name: fmt.Sprintf("%s_Linux_arm64.tar.gz", version),

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_sigstore_extensions.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

func main() {
	// Current signature extensions from the code
	currentExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore"}
	
	// Test files with different signature formats
	testFiles := []string{
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.minisig", 
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sign",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json",  // This should be detected but currently isn'"'"'t
		"package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json",     // This should be detected but currently isn'"'"'t
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz",                // Not a signature file
		"package-1.0.0.whl",                    // Not a signature file
	}
	
	fmt.Println("Testing current signature extension detection:")
	fmt.Printf("Current extensions: %v\n\n", currentExtensions)
	
	for _, testFile := range testFiles {
		isSignature := false
		for _, ext := range currentExtensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(testFile, ext) {
				isSignature = true
				break
			}
		}
		
		status := "✓ SIGNATURE"
		if !isSignature {
			status = "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
		}
		fmt.Printf("%-50s %s\n", testFile, status)
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\n" + strings.Repeat("=", 60))
	
	// Test with proposed fix
	proposedExtensions := append(currentExtensions, ".sigstore.json")
	fmt.Println("\nTesting with proposed fix (adding .sigstore.json):")
	fmt.Printf("Proposed extensions: %v\n\n", proposedExtensions)
	
	for _, testFile := range testFiles {
		isSignature := false
		for _, ext := range proposedExtensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(testFile, ext) {
				isSignature = true
				break
			}
		}
		
		status := "✓ SIGNATURE"
		if !isSignature {
			status = "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
		}
		fmt.Printf("%-50s %s\n", testFile, status)
	}
}'

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"
	"testing"

	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/checker"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/clients"
	"github.com/ossf/scorecard/v5/probes/releasesAreSigned"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("=== Testing sigstore.json signature detection ===\n")

	// Test 1: Direct string suffix matching
	testExtensions()

	// Test 2: Simulate the actual probe logic
	testProbeLogic()

	// Test 3: Edge cases
	testEdgeCases()

	fmt.Println("\n=== All tests completed successfully! ===")
}

func testExtensions() {
	fmt.Println("Test 1: Extension matching")
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 40))

	currentExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	testFiles := []string{
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.minisig",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sign",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json",
		"package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz",
		"package-1.0.0.whl",
	}

	for _, testFile := range testFiles {
		isSignature := false
		for _, ext := range currentExtensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(testFile, ext) {
				isSignature = true
				break
			}
		}

		status := "✓ SIGNATURE"
		if !isSignature {
			status = "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
		}
		fmt.Printf("%-50s %s\n", testFile, status)
	}
}

func testProbeLogic() {
	fmt.Println("\nTest 2: Simulating probe logic with test data")
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 40))

	// Create test data similar to what would be processed by the probe
	testData := &checker.RawResults{
		SignedReleasesResults: checker.SignedReleasesData{
			Releases: []clients.Release{
				{
					TagName: "v1.0.0",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.tar.gz"},
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json"},
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.whl"},
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json"},
					},
				},
				{
					TagName: "v0.9.0",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package-0.9.0.tar.gz"},
						{Name: "package-0.9.0.tar.gz.asc"},
					},
				},
				{
					TagName: "v0.8.0",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package-0.8.0.tar.gz"},
						{Name: "README.md"},
					},
				},
			},
		},
	}

	// Simulate the probe logic
	signatureExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	for _, release := range testData.SignedReleasesResults.Releases {
		signed := false
		for _, asset := range release.Assets {
			for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
				if strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
					fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✓ Found signature file: %s\n", release.TagName, asset.Name)
					signed = true
					break
				}
			}
			if signed {
				break
			}
		}
		
		if !signed {
			fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✗ No signature found\n", release.TagName)
		}
	}
}

func testEdgeCases() {
	fmt.Println("\nTest 3: Edge cases")
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 40))

	// Create edge case test data
	testData := &checker.RawResults{
		SignedReleasesResults: checker.SignedReleasesData{
			Releases: []clients.Release{
				{
					TagName: "edge-v1",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package.sigstore.json.backup"}, // This should NOT match
						{Name: "package.sigstore.JSON"},        // Case sensitive, should NOT match
						{Name: "package.json"},                 // Not a signature
					},
				},
				{
					TagName: "edge-v2", 
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package.sigstore.json"},        // This SHOULD match
						{Name: "package.minisig"},              // Should also match
					},
				},
			},
		},
	}

	signatureExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	for _, release := range testData.SignedReleasesResults.Releases {
		signed := false
		for _, asset := range release.Assets {
			for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
				if strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
					fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✓ Found signature file: %s\n", release.TagName, asset.Name)
					signed = true
					break
				}
			}
		}
		
		if !signed {
			fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✗ No signature found (correct behavior)\n", release.TagName)
		}
	}
}

// Helper function to run unit tests
func TestSignatureDetection(t *testing.T) {
	signatureExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	testCases := []struct {
		filename string
		expected bool
	}{
		{"package.tar.gz.sigstore.json", true},
		{"package.whl.sigstore.json", true},
		{"package.sigstore.json.backup", false},
		{"SIGSTORE.JSON", false}, // Case sensitive
		{"package.json", false},
		{"package.sigstore", true},
		{"package.asc", true},
	}
	
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		matched := false
		for _, ext := range signatureExtensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(tc.filename, ext) {
				matched = true
				break
			}
		}
		
		if matched != tc.expected {
			t.Errorf("File %s: expected %v, got %v", tc.filename, tc.expected, matched)
		}
	}
}'

import (

func testExtensions() {
	fmt.Println("Test 1: Extension matching")
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 40))

	currentExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	testFiles := []string{
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.minisig",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sign",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json",
		"package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json",
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz",
		"package-1.0.0.whl",
	}

	for _, testFile := range testFiles {
		isSignature := false
		for _, ext := range currentExtensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(testFile, ext) {
				isSignature = true
				break
			}
		}

		status := "✓ SIGNATURE"
		if !isSignature {
			status = "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
		}
		fmt.Printf("%-50s %s\n", testFile, status)
	}
}

func testProbeLogic() {
	fmt.Println("\nTest 2: Simulating probe logic with test data")
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 40))

	// Create test data similar to what would be processed by the probe
	testData := &checker.RawResults{
		SignedReleasesResults: checker.SignedReleasesData{
			Releases: []clients.Release{
				{
					TagName: "v1.0.0",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.tar.gz"},
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json"},
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.whl"},
						{Name: "package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json"},
					},
				},
				{
					TagName: "v0.9.0",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package-0.9.0.tar.gz"},
						{Name: "package-0.9.0.tar.gz.asc"},
					},
				},
				{
					TagName: "v0.8.0",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package-0.8.0.tar.gz"},
						{Name: "README.md"},
					},
				},
			},
		},
	}

	// Simulate the probe logic
	signatureExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	for _, release := range testData.SignedReleasesResults.Releases {
		signed := false
		for _, asset := range release.Assets {
			for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
				if strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
					fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✓ Found signature file: %s\n", release.TagName, asset.Name)
					signed = true
					break
				}
			}
			if signed {
				break
			}
		}
		
		if !signed {
			fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✗ No signature found\n", release.TagName)
		}
	}
}

func testEdgeCases() {
	fmt.Println("\nTest 3: Edge cases")
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 40))

	// Create edge case test data
	testData := &checker.RawResults{
		SignedReleasesResults: checker.SignedReleasesData{
			Releases: []clients.Release{
				{
					TagName: "edge-v1",
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package.sigstore.json.backup"}, // This should NOT match
						{Name: "package.sigstore.JSON"},        // Case sensitive, should NOT match
						{Name: "package.json"},                 // Not a signature
					},
				},
				{
					TagName: "edge-v2", 
					Assets: []clients.ReleaseAsset{
						{Name: "package.sigstore.json"},        // This SHOULD match
						{Name: "package.minisig"},              // Should also match
					},
				},
			},
		},
	}

	signatureExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	for _, release := range testData.SignedReleasesResults.Releases {
		signed := false
		for _, asset := range release.Assets {
			for _, suffix := range signatureExtensions {
				if strings.HasSuffix(asset.Name, suffix) {
					fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✓ Found signature file: %s\n", release.TagName, asset.Name)
					signed = true
					break
				}
			}
		}
		
		if !signed {
			fmt.Printf("Release %s: ✗ No signature found (correct behavior)\n", release.TagName)
		}
	}
}

// Helper function to run unit tests
func TestSignatureDetection(t *testing.T) {
	signatureExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	testCases := []struct {
		filename string
		expected bool
	}{
		{"package.tar.gz.sigstore.json", true},
		{"package.whl.sigstore.json", true},
		{"package.sigstore.json.backup", false},
		{"SIGSTORE.JSON", false}, // Case sensitive
		{"package.json", false},
		{"package.sigstore", true},
		{"package.asc", true},
	}
	
	for _, tc := range testCases {
		matched := false
		for _, ext := range signatureExtensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(tc.filename, ext) {
				matched = true
				break
			}
		}
		
		if matched != tc.expected {
			t.Errorf("File %s: expected %v, got %v", tc.filename, tc.expected, matched)
		}
	}

	testFiles := []string{
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",                       // Should match
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.minisig",                   // Should match
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",                       // Should match
		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sign",                      // Should match

		"package-1.0.0.tar.gz",                           // Should NOT match
		"package-1.0.0.whl",                              // Should NOT match
		"package.sigstore.json.backup",                   // Should NOT match
		"package.sigstore.JSON",                          // Should NOT match (case sensitive)
		"package.json",                                   // Should NOT match
	}

	fmt.Println("File extension detection test:")
	fmt.Println(strings.Repeat("-", 60))

	for _, testFile := range testFiles {
		isSignature := false

			if strings.HasSuffix(testFile, ext) {
				isSignature = true
				break
			}
		}

		// Determine expected result
		expectedSignature := false
		if strings.HasSuffix(testFile, ".asc") ||
		   strings.HasSuffix(testFile, ".minisig") ||

			status = "✗ WRONG"

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("=== Verifying sigstore.json fix ===\n")

	// Current signature extensions from the code
	signatureExtensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	// Test files
	testFiles := []string{
		"package.tar.gz.asc",
		"package.tar.gz.sigstore",
		"package.tar.gz.sigstore.json",
		"package.whl.sigstore.json",
		"package.txt",
		"package.json",
	}

	fmt.Println("Signature extensions:", signatureExtensions)
	fmt.Println("\nTesting files:")
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 50))
	
	allCorrect := true
	for _, filename := range testFiles {
		isSignature := false
		for _, ext := range signatureExtensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(filename, ext) {
				isSignature = true
				break
			}
		}
		
		// Determine expected result
		expected := false
		if strings.HasSuffix(filename, ".asc") ||
		   strings.HasSuffix(filename, ".minisig") ||
		   strings.HasSuffix(filename, ".sig") ||
		   strings.HasSuffix(filename, ".sign") ||
		   strings.HasSuffix(filename, ".sigstore") ||
		   strings.HasSuffix(filename, ".sigstore.json") {
			expected = true
		}
		
		status := "✓"
		if isSignature != expected {
			status = "✗"
			allCorrect = false
		}
		
		result := "Not Signature"
		if isSignature {
			result = "Signature"
		}
		
		fmt.Printf("%-30s %-15s %s\n", filename, result, status)
	}
	
	fmt.Println("-" + strings.Repeat("-", 50))
	if allCorrect {
		fmt.Println("✅ SUCCESS: All files correctly identified!")
		fmt.Println("✅ sigstore.json files are now recognized as signatures!")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("❌ FAILURE: Some files were incorrectly identified!")
	}
}'

package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing sigstore.json signature detection")
	
	extensions := []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
	
	testFiles := []string{
		"file.asc",
		"file.sigstore.json", 
		"file.tar.gz",
		"file.json",
	}
	
	for _, file := range testFiles {
		isSig := false
		for _, ext := range extensions {
			if strings.HasSuffix(file, ext) {
				isSig = true
				break
			}
		}
		fmt.Printf("%-20s: %v\n", file, isSig)
	}
	
	fmt.Println("\nExtensions:", extensions)
	fmt.Println("✅ sigstore.json is included!")
}
EOF

"""Test to verify that sigstore.json files are recognized as signature files."""

import os

def test_signature_detection():
    """Test the signature extension detection logic."""
    
    # Signature extensions after our fix
    signature_extensions = [".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"]
    
    # Test files
    test_files = [
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore",
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json",  # This should now be detected
        "package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json",      # This should now be detected
        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz",                 # Not a signature
        "package-1.0.0.whl",                    # Not a signature
        "package.sigstore.json.bak",           # Not a signature
        "package.json",                         # Not a signature
    ]
    
    print("Testing signature file detection after fix:")
    print("=" * 60)
    print(f"Signature extensions: {signature_extensions}")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    all_tests_passed = True
    
    for test_file in test_files:
        is_signature = False
        for ext in signature_extensions:
            if test_file.endswith(ext):
                is_signature = True
                break
        
        # Determine expected result
        expected = any(test_file.endswith(ext) for ext in signature_extensions)
        
        status = "✓ PASS" if is_signature == expected else "✗ FAIL"
        if is_signature != expected:
            all_tests_passed = False
        
        sig_status = "SIGNATURE" if is_signature else "NOT SIGNATURE"
        print(f"{test_file:40} {sig_status:12} {status}")
    
    print("-" * 60)
    if all_tests_passed:
        print("✅ All tests passed! sigstore.json files are correctly recognized.")
    else:
        print("❌ Some tests failed!")
    
    return all_tests_passed

def check_implementation():
    """Check that the actual implementation includes the fix."""
    
    print("\nChecking implementation files:")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # Check the actual implementation file
    impl_file = "/testbed/probes/releasesAreSigned/impl.go"
    
    if os.path.exists(impl_file):
        with open(impl_file, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
            
        if '"'"'".sigstore.json"'"'"' in content:
            print("✅ sigstore.json is present in the implementation file")
            
            # Find the signature extensions line
            lines = content.split('"'"'\n'"'"')
            for i, line in enumerate(lines):
                if '"'"'signatureExtensions'"'"' in line:
                    print(f"\nSignature extensions line ({i+1}): {line.strip()}")
                    break
        else:
            print("❌ sigstore.json is NOT present in the implementation file")
            
    # Check if tests include sigstore.json
    test_file = "/testbed/checks/signed_releases_test.go"
    
    if os.path.exists(test_file):
        with open(test_file, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
            
        if '"'"'sigstore.json'"'"' in content:
            print("✅ sigstore.json is present in test cases")
        else:
            print("❌ sigstore.json is NOT present in test cases")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("Verifying sigstore.json signature detection fix\n")
    
    test_passed = test_signature_detection()
    check_implementation()
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    if test_passed:
        print("✅ SUCCESS: The fix has been properly implemented!")
        print("   Python projects using sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python")
        print("   will now correctly pass the Signed-Releases check.")
    else:
        print("❌ FAILURE: The fix needs more work.")
    
    exit(0 if test_passed else 1)'

+# Summary of Changes for sigstore.json Support
+
+## Problem
+The `Signed-Releases` check was not recognizing `.sigstore.json` files produced by the sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python GitHub Action, causing Python projects using this official sigstore GitHub Action to fail the Signed-Releases check even when they had valid sigstore signatures.
+
+## Solution
+Added `.sigstore.json` to the list of recognized signature file extensions.
+
+## Changes Made
+
+### 1. Modified `/testbed/probes/releasesAreSigned/impl.go`
+**Line 44**: Added `.sigstore.json` to the `signatureExtensions` slice:
+```go
+var signatureExtensions = []string{".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"}
+```
+
+### 2. Added Test Case in `/testbed/checks/signed_releases_test.go`
+Added a new test case to verify that `.sigstore.json` files are properly recognized:
+- Test name: "Releases with assets with signed artifacts-sigstore.json"
+- This test ensures that files ending with `.sigstore.json` are treated as valid signatures
+
+## Testing
+
+### Manual Verification
+Created a verification script that confirms:
+- `.sigstore.json` files are correctly identified as signature files
+- All existing signature extensions continue to work
+- Non-signature files are correctly ignored
+- Edge cases are handled properly
+
+### Automated Tests
+- All existing tests continue to pass
+- New test case for `.sigstore.json` extension passes
+- Probe-level tests continue to pass
+
+## Impact
+This minimal change ensures that:
+1. Python projects using the official sigstore GitHub Action will now correctly pass the Signed-Releases check
+2. The change is backward compatible - all existing signature types continue to work
+3. No breaking changes to the API or existing functionality
+
+The fix specifically addresses the issue described in the PR where repositories like https://github.com/mark-adams/python-test-groups would now correctly show a score of 8 (instead of 0) for the Signed-Releases check.
\ No newline at end of file

+isSignature = true

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Test script to verify sigstore.json detection functionality."""

+def test_extensions():
+    # Current signature extensions from the code

+

+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.minisig", 
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sign",

+        "package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json",     # This should be detected but currently isn't
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz",                # Not a signature file
+        "package-1.0.0.whl",                    # Not a signature file
+    ]
+    
+    print("Testing current signature extension detection:")
+    print("Current extensions:", current_extensions)
+    print()
+    
+    for test_file in test_files:
+        is_signature = False
+        for ext in current_extensions:
+            if test_file.endswith(ext):
+                is_signature = True
+                break
+        
+        status = "✓ SIGNATURE" if is_signature else "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
+        print(f"{test_file:50} {status}")
+    
+    print("\n" + "="*60)
+    
+    # Test with proposed fix
+    proposed_extensions = current_extensions + [".sigstore.json"]
+    print("\nTesting with proposed fix (adding .sigstore.json):")
+    print("Proposed extensions:", proposed_extensions)
+    print()
+

+        is_signature = False
+        for ext in proposed_extensions:
+            if test_file.endswith(ext):
+                is_signature = True
+                break
+        
+        status = "✓ SIGNATURE" if is_signature else "✗ NOT SIGNATURE"
+        print(f"{test_file:50} {status}")

+    test_extensions()

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Test to verify that sigstore.json files are recognized as signature files."""
+
+import os
+
+def test_signature_detection():
+    """Test the signature extension detection logic."""
+    
+    # Signature extensions after our fix
+    signature_extensions = [".asc", ".minisig", ".sig", ".sign", ".sigstore", ".sigstore.json"]
+    
+    # Test files
+    test_files = [
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.asc",
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sig",
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore",
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz.sigstore.json",  # This should now be detected
+        "package-1.0.0.whl.sigstore.json",      # This should now be detected
+        "package-1.0.0.tar.gz",                 # Not a signature
+        "package-1.0.0.whl",                    # Not a signature
+        "package.sigstore.json.bak",           # Not a signature
+        "package.json",                         # Not a signature
+    ]
+    
+    print("Testing signature file detection after fix:")
+    print("=" * 60)
+    print(f"Signature extensions: {signature_extensions}")
+    print("-" * 60)
+    
+    all_tests_passed = True
+    
+    for test_file in test_files:
+        is_signature = False
+        for ext in signature_extensions:
+            if test_file.endswith(ext):
+                is_signature = True
+                break
+        
+        # Determine expected result
+        expected = any(test_file.endswith(ext) for ext in signature_extensions)
+        
+        status = "✓ PASS" if is_signature == expected else "✗ FAIL"
+        if is_signature != expected:
+            all_tests_passed = False
+        
+        sig_status = "SIGNATURE" if is_signature else "NOT SIGNATURE"
+        print(f"{test_file:40} {sig_status:12} {status}")
+    
+    print("-" * 60)
+    if all_tests_passed:
+        print("✅ All tests passed! sigstore.json files are correctly recognized.")
+    else:
+        print("❌ Some tests failed!")
+    
+    return all_tests_passed
+
+def check_implementation():
+    """Check that the actual implementation includes the fix."""
+    
+    print("\nChecking implementation files:")
+    print("=" * 60)
+    
+    # Check the actual implementation file
+    impl_file = "/testbed/probes/releasesAreSigned/impl.go"
+    
+    if os.path.exists(impl_file):
+        with open(impl_file, 'r') as f:
+            content = f.read()
+            
+        if '".sigstore.json"' in content:
+            print("✅ sigstore.json is present in the implementation file")
+            
+            # Find the signature extensions line
+            lines = content.split('\n')
+            for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+                if 'signatureExtensions' in line:
+                    print(f"\nSignature extensions line ({i+1}): {line.strip()}")
+                    break
+        else:
+            print("❌ sigstore.json is NOT present in the implementation file")
+            
+    # Check if tests include sigstore.json
+    test_file = "/testbed/checks/signed_releases_test.go"
+    
+    if os.path.exists(test_file):
+        with open(test_file, 'r') as f:
+            content = f.read()
+            
+        if 'sigstore.json' in content:
+            print("✅ sigstore.json is present in test cases")
+        else:
+            print("❌ sigstore.json is NOT present in test cases")
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    print("Verifying sigstore.json signature detection fix\n")
+    
+    test_passed = test_signature_detection()
+    check_implementation()
+    
+    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
+    if test_passed:
+        print("✅ SUCCESS: The fix has been properly implemented!")
+        print("   Python projects using sigstore/gh-action-sigstore-python")
+        print("   will now correctly pass the Signed-Releases check.")
+    else:
+        print("❌ FAILURE: The fix needs more work.")
+    
+    exit(0 if test_passed else 1)
